# <a name="routing-in-aspnet-core"></a><span data-ttu-id="d429d-103">Routage dans ASP.NET Core</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-103">Routing in ASP.NET Core</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d429d-104">Par [Ryan Nowak](https://github.com/rynowak), [Kirk Larkin](https://twitter.com/serpent5)et [Rick Anderson](https://twitter.com/RickAndMSFT)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-104">By [Ryan Nowak](https://github.com/rynowak), [Kirk Larkin](https://twitter.com/serpent5), and [Rick Anderson](https://twitter.com/RickAndMSFT)</span></span>

::: moniker range=">= aspnetcore-3.0"

<span data-ttu-id="d429d-105">Le routage est responsable de la mise en correspondance des demandes HTTP entrantes et de la distribution de ces requêtes aux points de terminaison exécutables de l’application.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-105">Routing is responsible for matching incoming HTTP requests and dispatching those requests to the app's executable endpoints.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-106">Les [points de terminaison](#endpoint) sont les unités de code de gestion des requêtes exécutables de l’application.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-106">[Endpoints](#endpoint) are the app's units of executable request-handling code.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-107">Les points de terminaison sont définis dans l’application et configurés au démarrage de l’application.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-107">Endpoints are defined in the app and configured when the app starts.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-108">Le processus de correspondance de point de terminaison peut extraire des valeurs de l’URL de la demande et fournir ces valeurs pour le traitement des demandes.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-108">The endpoint matching process can extract values from the request's URL and provide those values for request processing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-109">À l’aide des informations de point de terminaison de l’application, le routage est également en mesure de générer des URL qui mappent aux points de terminaison.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-109">Using endpoint information from the app, routing is also able to generate URLs that map to endpoints.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d429d-110">Les applications peuvent configurer le routage à l’aide de :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-110">Apps can configure routing using:</span></span>

- <span data-ttu-id="d429d-111">Controllers</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-111">Controllers</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="d429d-112">RazorPages</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-112">Razor Pages</span></span>
- SignalR
- <span data-ttu-id="d429d-113">Services gRPC</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-113">gRPC Services</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="d429d-114">[Intergiciel (middleware](xref:fundamentals/middleware/index) ) prenant en charge les points de terminaison, tels que les [contrôles d’intégrité](xref:host-and-deploy/health-checks).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-114">Endpoint-enabled [middleware](xref:fundamentals/middleware/index) such as [Health Checks](xref:host-and-deploy/health-checks).</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="d429d-115">Délégués et expressions lambda inscrits avec le routage.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-115">Delegates and lambdas registered with routing.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d429d-116">Ce document traite des détails de bas niveau du routage de ASP.NET Core.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-116">This document covers low-level details of ASP.NET Core routing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-117">Pour plus d’informations sur la configuration du routage :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-117">For information on configuring routing:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="d429d-118">Pour les contrôleurs, consultez <xref:mvc/controllers/routing> .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-118">For controllers, see <xref:mvc/controllers/routing>.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="d429d-119">Pour les Razor conventions de pages, consultez <xref:razor-pages/razor-pages-conventions> .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-119">For Razor Pages conventions, see <xref:razor-pages/razor-pages-conventions>.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d429d-120">Le système de routage des points de terminaison décrit dans ce document s’applique à ASP.NET Core 3,0 et versions ultérieures.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-120">The endpoint routing system described in this document applies to ASP.NET Core 3.0 and later.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-121">Pour plus d’informations sur le système de routage précédent basé sur <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter> , sélectionnez la version ASP.NET Core 2,1 à l’aide de l’une des approches suivantes :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-121">For information on the previous routing system based on <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouter>, select the ASP.NET Core 2.1 version using one of the following approaches:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="d429d-122">Sélecteur de version d’une version précédente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-122">The version selector for a previous version.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="d429d-123">Sélectionnez [ASP.net Core routage 2,1](https://docs.microsoft.com/aspnet/core/fundamentals/routing?view=aspnetcore-2.1).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-123">Select [ASP.NET Core 2.1 routing](https://docs.microsoft.com/aspnet/core/fundamentals/routing?view=aspnetcore-2.1).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d429d-124">[Afficher ou télécharger l’exemple de code](https://github.com/aspnet/AspNetCore.Docs/tree/master/aspnetcore/fundamentals/routing/samples/3.x) ([procédure de téléchargement](xref:index#how-to-download-a-sample))</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-124">[View or download sample code](https://github.com/aspnet/AspNetCore.Docs/tree/master/aspnetcore/fundamentals/routing/samples/3.x) ([how to download](xref:index#how-to-download-a-sample))</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d429d-125">Les exemples de téléchargement de ce document sont activés par une `Startup` classe spécifique.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-125">The download samples for this document are enabled by a specific `Startup` class.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-126">Pour exécuter un exemple spécifique, modifiez *Program.cs* pour appeler la `Startup` classe souhaitée.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-126">To run a specific sample, modify *Program.cs* to call the desired `Startup` class.</span></span>

## <a name="routing-basics"></a><span data-ttu-id="d429d-127">Concepts de base du routage</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-127">Routing basics</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d429d-128">Tous les modèles de ASP.NET Core incluent le routage dans le code généré.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-128">All ASP.NET Core templates include routing in the generated code.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-129">Le routage est inscrit dans le pipeline de l' [intergiciel (middleware](xref:fundamentals/middleware/index) ) dans `Startup.Configure` .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-129">Routing is registered in the [middleware](xref:fundamentals/middleware/index) pipeline in `Startup.Configure`.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d429d-130">Le code suivant illustre un exemple de routage de base :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-130">The following code shows a basic example of routing:</span></span>

[!code-csharp[](routing/samples/3.x/RoutingSample/Startup.cs?name=snippet&highlight=8,10)]

<span data-ttu-id="d429d-131">Le routage utilise une paire d’intergiciels (middleware), inscrite par <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRoutingApplicationBuilderExtensions.UseRouting*> et <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRoutingApplicationBuilderExtensions.UseEndpoints*> :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-131">Routing uses a pair of middleware, registered by <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRoutingApplicationBuilderExtensions.UseRouting*> and <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRoutingApplicationBuilderExtensions.UseEndpoints*>:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="d429d-132">`UseRouting`Ajoute la correspondance d’itinéraire au pipeline de l’intergiciel (middleware).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-132">`UseRouting` adds route matching to the middleware pipeline.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-133">Cet intergiciel (middleware) examine l’ensemble des points de terminaison définis dans l’application et sélectionne la [meilleure correspondance](#urlm) en fonction de la demande.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-133">This middleware looks at the set of endpoints defined in the app, and selects the [best match](#urlm) based on the request.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="d429d-134">`UseEndpoints`Ajoute l’exécution du point de terminaison au pipeline d’intergiciel (middleware).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-134">`UseEndpoints` adds endpoint execution to the middleware pipeline.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-135">Il exécute le délégué associé au point de terminaison sélectionné.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-135">It runs the delegate associated with the selected endpoint.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d429d-136">L’exemple précédent comprend un seul *itinéraire vers le point de terminaison de code* à l’aide de la méthode [MapGet](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRouteBuilderExtensions.MapGet*) :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-136">The preceding example includes a single *route to code* endpoint using the [MapGet](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRouteBuilderExtensions.MapGet*) method:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="d429d-137">Quand une `GET` requête HTTP est envoyée à l’URL racine `/` :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-137">When an HTTP `GET` request is sent to the root URL `/`:</span></span>
  * <span data-ttu-id="d429d-138">Le délégué de requête indiqué s’exécute.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-138">The request delegate shown executes.</span></span>
  * <span data-ttu-id="d429d-139">`Hello World!`est écrit dans la réponse HTTP.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-139">`Hello World!` is written to the HTTP response.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-140">Par défaut, l’URL racine `/` est `https://localhost:5001/` .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-140">By default, the root URL `/` is `https://localhost:5001/`.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="d429d-141">Si la méthode de demande n’est pas `GET` ou si l’URL racine n’est pas `/` , aucun itinéraire ne correspond et un http 404 est retourné.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-141">If the request method is not `GET` or the root URL is not `/`, no route matches and an HTTP 404 is returned.</span></span>

### <a name="endpoint"></a><span data-ttu-id="d429d-142">Point de terminaison</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-142">Endpoint</span></span>

<a name="endpoint"></a>

<span data-ttu-id="d429d-143">La `MapGet` méthode est utilisée pour définir un **point de terminaison**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-143">The `MapGet` method is used to define an **endpoint**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-144">Un point de terminaison est un point qui peut être :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-144">An endpoint is something that can be:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="d429d-145">Sélectionné en faisant correspondre l’URL et la méthode HTTP.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-145">Selected, by matching the URL and HTTP method.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="d429d-146">Exécuté, en exécutant le délégué.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-146">Executed, by running the delegate.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d429d-147">Les points de terminaison qui peuvent être mis en correspondance et exécutés par l’application sont configurés dans `UseEndpoints` .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-147">Endpoints that can be matched and executed by the app are configured in `UseEndpoints`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-148">Par exemple, <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRouteBuilderExtensions.MapGet*> , <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRouteBuilderExtensions.MapPost*> et les [méthodes similaires](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRouteBuilderExtensions) connectent les délégués de demande au système de routage.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-148">For example, <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRouteBuilderExtensions.MapGet*>, <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRouteBuilderExtensions.MapPost*>, and [similar methods](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRouteBuilderExtensions) connect request delegates to the routing system.</span></span>
<span data-ttu-id="d429d-149">Des méthodes supplémentaires peuvent être utilisées pour connecter les fonctionnalités de ASP.NET Core Framework au système de routage :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-149">Additional methods can be used to connect ASP.NET Core framework features to the routing system:</span></span>
- <span data-ttu-id="d429d-150">[Mapper Razor des pages pour les Razor pages](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.RazorPagesEndpointRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRazorPages*)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-150">[MapRazorPages for Razor Pages](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.RazorPagesEndpointRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRazorPages*)</span></span>
- [<span data-ttu-id="d429d-151">MapControllers pour les contrôleurs</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-151">MapControllers for controllers</span></span>](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.ControllerEndpointRouteBuilderExtensions.MapControllers*)
- <span data-ttu-id="d429d-152">[MapHub \<THub> pourSignalR](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.SignalR.HubRouteBuilder.MapHub*)</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-152">[MapHub\<THub> for SignalR](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.SignalR.HubRouteBuilder.MapHub*)</span></span> 
- [<span data-ttu-id="d429d-153">MapGrpcService \<TService> pour gRPC</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-153">MapGrpcService\<TService> for gRPC</span></span>](xref:grpc/aspnetcore)

<span data-ttu-id="d429d-154">L’exemple suivant illustre le routage avec un modèle d’itinéraire plus sophistiqué :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-154">The following example shows routing with a more sophisticated route template:</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d429d-155">La chaîne `/hello/{name:alpha}` est un **modèle de routage**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-155">The string `/hello/{name:alpha}` is a **route template**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-156">Il permet de configurer la mise en correspondance du point de terminaison.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-156">It is used to configure how the endpoint is matched.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-157">Dans ce cas, le modèle correspond à :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-157">In this case, the template matches:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="d429d-158">Une URL telle que`/hello/Ryan`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-158">A URL like `/hello/Ryan`</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="d429d-159">Tout chemin d’accès d’URL qui commence par `/hello/` , suivi d’une séquence de caractères alphabétiques.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-159">Any URL path that begins with `/hello/` followed by a sequence of alphabetic characters.</span></span>  <span data-ttu-id="d429d-160">`:alpha`applique une contrainte d’itinéraire qui correspond uniquement aux caractères alphabétiques.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-160">`:alpha` applies a route constraint that matches only alphabetic characters.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-161">Les [contraintes de routage](#route-constraint-reference) sont expliquées plus loin dans ce document.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-161">[Route constraints](#route-constraint-reference) are explained later in this document.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d429d-162">Le deuxième segment du chemin d’URL `{name:alpha}` :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-162">The second segment of the URL path, `{name:alpha}`:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="d429d-163">Est lié au `name` paramètre.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-163">Is bound to the `name` parameter.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="d429d-164">Est capturé et stocké dans [HttpRequest. RouteValues](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.HttpRequest.RouteValues*).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-164">Is captured and stored in [HttpRequest.RouteValues](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.HttpRequest.RouteValues*).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d429d-165">Le système de routage des points de terminaison décrit dans ce document est nouveau à partir de ASP.NET Core 3,0.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-165">The endpoint routing system described in this document is new as of ASP.NET Core 3.0.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-166">Toutefois, toutes les versions de ASP.NET Core prennent en charge le même jeu de fonctionnalités de modèle de routage et de contraintes de routage.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-166">However, all versions of ASP.NET Core support the same set of route template features and route constraints.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d429d-168">L’exemple précédent montre comment :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-168">The preceding example demonstrates how:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="d429d-169">L’intergiciel d’autorisation peut être utilisé avec le routage.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-169">The authorization middleware can be used with routing.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="d429d-170">Les points de terminaison peuvent être utilisés pour configurer le comportement d’autorisation.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-170">Endpoints can be used to configure authorization behavior.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d429d-171">L' <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.HealthCheckEndpointRouteBuilderExtensions.MapHealthChecks*> appel ajoute un point de terminaison de contrôle d’intégrité.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-171">The <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.HealthCheckEndpointRouteBuilderExtensions.MapHealthChecks*> call adds a health check endpoint.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-172">Le chaînage <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.AuthorizationEndpointConventionBuilderExtensions.RequireAuthorization*> sur cet appel joint une stratégie d’autorisation au point de terminaison.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-172">Chaining <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.AuthorizationEndpointConventionBuilderExtensions.RequireAuthorization*> on to this call attaches an authorization policy to the endpoint.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d429d-173"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.AuthAppBuilderExtensions.UseAuthentication*>L’appel de et <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.AuthorizationAppBuilderExtensions.UseAuthorization*> ajoute l’intergiciel (middleware) d’authentification et d’autorisation.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-173">Calling <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.AuthAppBuilderExtensions.UseAuthentication*> and <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.AuthorizationAppBuilderExtensions.UseAuthorization*> adds the authentication and authorization middleware.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-174">Ces intergiciels sont placés entre <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRoutingApplicationBuilderExtensions.UseRouting*> et `UseEndpoints` afin de pouvoir :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-174">These middleware are placed between <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRoutingApplicationBuilderExtensions.UseRouting*> and `UseEndpoints` so that they can:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="d429d-175">Consultez le point de terminaison sélectionné par `UseRouting` .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-175">See which endpoint was selected by `UseRouting`.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="d429d-176">Appliquez une stratégie d’autorisation avant <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRoutingApplicationBuilderExtensions.UseEndpoints*> les distributions au point de terminaison.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-176">Apply an authorization policy before <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRoutingApplicationBuilderExtensions.UseEndpoints*> dispatches to the endpoint.</span></span>

<a name="metadata"></a>

### <a name="endpoint-metadata"></a><span data-ttu-id="d429d-177">Métadonnées de point de terminaison</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-177">Endpoint metadata</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d429d-178">Dans l’exemple précédent, il existe deux points de terminaison, mais seul le point de terminaison de contrôle d’intégrité a une stratégie d’autorisation attachée.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-178">In the preceding example, there are two endpoints, but only the health check endpoint has an authorization policy attached.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-179">Si la demande correspond au point de terminaison de contrôle d’intégrité, `/healthz` une vérification d’autorisation est effectuée.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-179">If the request matches the health check endpoint, `/healthz`, an authorization check is performed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-180">Cela démontre que des données supplémentaires peuvent être attachées aux points de terminaison.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-180">This demonstrates that endpoints can have extra data attached to them.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-181">Ces données supplémentaires sont appelées **métadonnées**de point de terminaison :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-181">This extra data is called endpoint **metadata**:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="d429d-182">Les métadonnées peuvent être traitées par un intergiciel (middleware) qui prend en charge le routage.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-182">The metadata can be processed by routing-aware middleware.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="d429d-183">Les métadonnées peuvent être de n’importe quel type .NET.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-183">The metadata can be of any .NET type.</span></span>

## <a name="routing-concepts"></a><span data-ttu-id="d429d-184">Concepts de routage</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-184">Routing concepts</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d429d-185">Le système de routage s’appuie sur le pipeline de l’intergiciel (middleware) en ajoutant le puissant concept de **point de terminaison** .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-185">The routing system builds on top of the middleware pipeline by adding the powerful **endpoint** concept.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-186">Les points de terminaison représentent les unités de la fonctionnalité de l’application qui sont distinctes les unes des autres en termes de routage, d’autorisation et de tout nombre de systèmes de ASP.NET Core.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-186">Endpoints represent units of the app's functionality that are distinct from each other in terms of routing, authorization, and any number of ASP.NET Core's systems.</span></span>

<a name="endpoint"></a>

### <a name="aspnet-core-endpoint-definition"></a><span data-ttu-id="d429d-187">Définition de point de terminaison ASP.NET Core</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-187">ASP.NET Core endpoint definition</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d429d-188">Un point de terminaison de ASP.NET Core est :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-188">An ASP.NET Core endpoint is:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="d429d-189">Exécutable : a <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.Endpoint.RequestDelegate> .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-189">Executable: Has a <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.Endpoint.RequestDelegate>.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="d429d-190">Extensible : a une collection de [métadonnées](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.Endpoint.Metadata*) .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-190">Extensible: Has a [Metadata](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.Endpoint.Metadata*) collection.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="d429d-191">Sélectionnable : le cas échéant, contient des [informations de routage](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteEndpoint.RoutePattern*).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-191">Selectable: Optionally, has [routing information](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteEndpoint.RoutePattern*).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="d429d-192">Énumérable : la collection de points de terminaison peut être listée en extrayant le <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.EndpointDataSource> de [di](xref:fundamentals/dependency-injection).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-192">Enumerable: The collection of endpoints can be listed by retrieving the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.EndpointDataSource> from [DI](xref:fundamentals/dependency-injection).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d429d-193">Le code suivant montre comment récupérer et inspecter le point de terminaison correspondant à la requête actuelle :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-193">The following code shows how to retrieve and inspect the endpoint matching the current request:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="d429d-207">Si une correspondance est trouvée, le point de terminaison n’a pas la valeur null entre `UseRouting` et <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRoutingApplicationBuilderExtensions.UseEndpoints*> .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-207">If a match is found, the endpoint is non-null between `UseRouting` and <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRoutingApplicationBuilderExtensions.UseEndpoints*>.</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="d429d-210">L’intergiciel (middleware) après l' `UseEndpoints` exécution uniquement quand aucune correspondance n’est trouvée.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-210">The middleware after `UseEndpoints` execute only when no match is found.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d429d-211">L' `UseRouting` intergiciel utilise la méthode [SetEndpoint](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.EndpointHttpContextExtensions.SetEndpoint*) pour attacher le point de terminaison au contexte actuel.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-211">The `UseRouting` middleware uses the [SetEndpoint](xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.EndpointHttpContextExtensions.SetEndpoint*) method to attach the endpoint to the current context.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-212">Il est possible de remplacer l' `UseRouting` intergiciel par une logique personnalisée tout en bénéficiant des avantages de l’utilisation des points de terminaison.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-212">It's possible to replace the `UseRouting` middleware with custom logic and still get the benefits of using endpoints.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-213">Les points de terminaison sont une primitive de bas niveau, comme l’intergiciel (middleware), et ne sont pas couplés à l’implémentation du routage.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-213">Endpoints are a low-level primitive like middleware, and aren't coupled to the routing implementation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-214">La plupart des applications n’ont pas besoin d’être remplacées `UseRouting` par une logique personnalisée.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-214">Most apps don't need to replace `UseRouting` with custom logic.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d429d-215">L' `UseEndpoints` intergiciel (middleware) est conçu pour être utilisé en tandem avec l' `UseRouting` intergiciel (middleware).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-215">The `UseEndpoints` middleware is designed to be used in tandem with the `UseRouting` middleware.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-216">La logique de base pour exécuter un point de terminaison n’est pas compliquée.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-216">The core logic to execute an endpoint isn't complicated.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-217">Utilisez <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.EndpointHttpContextExtensions.GetEndpoint*> pour récupérer le point de terminaison, puis appelez sa <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.Endpoint.RequestDelegate> propriété.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-217">Use <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.EndpointHttpContextExtensions.GetEndpoint*> to retrieve the endpoint, and then invoke its <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.Endpoint.RequestDelegate> property.</span></span>

    * <span data-ttu-id="d429d-221">En général, l’intergiciel s’affiche avant que le routage ne modifie une propriété de la requête, telle que <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.RewriteBuilderExtensions.UseRewriter*> , <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.HttpMethodOverrideExtensions.UseHttpMethodOverride*> ou <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.UsePathBaseExtensions.UsePathBase*> .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-221">Usually middleware that appears before routing modifies some property of the request, such as <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.RewriteBuilderExtensions.UseRewriter*>, <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.HttpMethodOverrideExtensions.UseHttpMethodOverride*>, or <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.UsePathBaseExtensions.UsePathBase*>.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="d429d-222">L’intergiciel peut s’exécuter entre `UseRouting` et <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRoutingApplicationBuilderExtensions.UseEndpoints*> pour traiter les résultats du routage avant l’exécution du point de terminaison.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-222">Middleware can run between `UseRouting` and <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRoutingApplicationBuilderExtensions.UseEndpoints*> to process the results of routing before the endpoint is executed.</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="d429d-223">Intergiciel qui s’exécute entre `UseRouting` et `UseEndpoints` :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-223">Middleware that runs between `UseRouting` and `UseEndpoints`:</span></span>
      * <span data-ttu-id="d429d-224">Inspecte généralement les métadonnées pour comprendre les points de terminaison.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-224">Usually inspects metadata to understand the endpoints.</span></span>
      * <span data-ttu-id="d429d-225">Prend souvent des décisions de sécurité, comme c’est le cas par `UseAuthorization` et `UseCors` .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-225">Often makes security decisions, as done by `UseAuthorization` and `UseCors`.</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="d429d-226">La combinaison d’intergiciels (middleware) et de métadonnées permet de configurer des stratégies par point de terminaison.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-226">The combination of middleware and metadata allows configuring policies per-endpoint.</span></span>

*audit log* of access to sensitive data to the console.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-229">L’intergiciel peut être configuré pour *auditer* un point de terminaison avec les metadata.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-230">Cet exemple illustre un modèle d' *abonnement* dans lequel seuls les points de terminaison marqués comme sensibles sont audités.</span><span du point de terminaison est flexible.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-232">The endpoint metadata system is flexible.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-233">Cette logique peut être conçue de la manière qui convient le mieux au cas d’usage.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-233">This logic could be designed in whatever way suits the use case.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d429d-239">Les métadonnées de la stratégie d’audit `AuditPolicyAttribute` sont définies en tant que `Attribute` pour une utilisation plus facile avec les infrastructures basées sur des classes telles que les contrôleurs et SignalR .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-239">The audit policy metadata `AuditPolicyAttribute` is defined as an `Attribute` for easier use with class-based frameworks such as controllers and SignalR.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-240">Lors de l’utilisation *de l’itinéraire vers le code*:</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-240">When using *route to code*:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="d429d-241">Les métadonnées sont jointes à une API de générateur.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-241">Metadata is attached with a builder API.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="d429d-242">Les infrastructures basées sur des classes incluent tous les attributs de la méthode et de la classe correspondantes lors de la création de points de terminaison.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-242">Class-based frameworks include all attributes on the corresponding method and class when creating endpoints.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d429d-243">Les meilleures pratiques pour les types de métadonnées sont de les définir comme des interfaces ou des attributs.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-243">The best practices for metadata types are to define them either as interfaces or attributes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-244">Les interfaces et les attributs permettent de réutiliser le code.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-244">Interfaces and attributes allow code reuse.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-245">Le système de métadonnées est flexible et n’impose aucune restriction.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-245">The metadata system is flexible and doesn't impose any limitations.</span></span>

<a name="tm"></a>

### <a name="comparing-a-terminal-middleware-and-routing"></a><span data-ttu-id="d429d-246">Comparaison entre un intergiciel et un routage de terminaux</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-246">Comparing a terminal middleware and routing</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d429d-247">L’exemple de code suivant compare l’utilisation de l’intergiciel avec le routage :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-247">The following code sample contrasts using middleware with using routing:</span></span>

[!code-csharp[](routing/samples/3.x/RoutingSample/TerminalMiddlewareStartup.cs?name=snippet)]

<span data-ttu-id="d429d-248">Le style d’intergiciel (middleware) présenté avec est l’intergiciel (middleware) de `Approach 1:` **Terminal**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-248">The style of middleware shown with `Approach 1:` is **terminal middleware**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-249">Il s’agit de l’intergiciel (middleware) Terminal Server, car il effectue une opération de correspondance :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-249">It's called terminal middleware because it does a matching operation:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="d429d-250">L’opération de correspondance dans l’exemple précédent concerne `Path == "/"` l’intergiciel et le `Path == "/Movie"` routage.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-250">The matching operation in the preceding sample is `Path == "/"` for the middleware and `Path == "/Movie"` for routing.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="d429d-251">Lorsqu’une correspondance est réussie, elle exécute certaines fonctionnalités et retourne, plutôt que d’appeler l' `next` intergiciel (middleware).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-251">When a match is successful, it executes some functionality and returns, rather than invoking the `next` middleware.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d429d-252">Il s’agit de l’intergiciel (middleware) Terminal Server, car il met fin à la recherche, exécute certaines fonctionnalités, puis retourne.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-252">It's called terminal middleware because it terminates the search, executes some functionality, and then returns.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d429d-253">Comparaison entre un intergiciel et un routage de terminaux :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-253">Comparing a terminal middleware and routing:</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="d429d-254">Les deux approches permettent d’arrêter le pipeline de traitement :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-254">Both approaches allow terminating the processing pipeline:</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="d429d-255">L’intergiciel termine le pipeline en retournant plutôt qu’en appelant `next` .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-255">Middleware terminates the pipeline by returning rather than invoking `next`.</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="d429d-256">Les points de terminaison sont toujours des terminaux.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-256">Endpoints are always terminal.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="d429d-257">L’intergiciel (middleware) Terminal permet de positionner l’intergiciel (middleware) à un emplacement arbitraire dans le pipeline :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-257">Terminal middleware allows positioning the middleware at an arbitrary place in the pipeline:</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="d429d-258">Les points de terminaison s’exécutent à la position de <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRoutingApplicationBuilderExtensions.UseEndpoints*> .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-258">Endpoints execute at the position of <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.EndpointRoutingApplicationBuilderExtensions.UseEndpoints*>.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="d429d-259">L’intergiciel (middleware) Terminal permet au code arbitraire de déterminer quand l’intergiciel correspond à :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-259">Terminal middleware allows arbitrary code to determine when the middleware matches:</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="d429d-260">Le code de correspondance d’itinéraire personnalisé peut être détaillé et difficile à écrire correctement.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-260">Custom route matching code can be verbose and difficult to write correctly.</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="d429d-261">Le routage fournit des solutions simples pour les applications classiques.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-261">Routing provides straightforward solutions for typical apps.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-262">La plupart des applications n’ont pas besoin de code de correspondance d’itinéraire personnalisé.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-262">Most apps don't require custom route matching code.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="d429d-263">Interface des points de terminaison avec un intergiciel (middleware) tel que `UseAuthorization` et `UseCors` .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-263">Endpoints interface with middleware such as `UseAuthorization` and `UseCors`.</span></span>
    * <span data-ttu-id="d429d-264">L’utilisation d’un intergiciel (middleware) terminal avec `UseAuthorization` ou `UseCors` nécessite une interface manuelle avec le système d’autorisation.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-264">Using a terminal middleware with `UseAuthorization` or `UseCors` requires manual interfacing with the authorization system.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d429d-265">Un [point de terminaison](#endpoint) définit les deux :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-265">An [endpoint](#endpoint) defines both:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="d429d-266">Délégué pour traiter les demandes.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-266">A delegate to process requests.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="d429d-267">Collection de métadonnées arbitraires.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-267">A collection of arbitrary metadata.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-268">Les métadonnées sont utilisées pour implémenter des problèmes transversaux en fonction des stratégies et de la configuration attachées à chaque point de terminaison.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-268">The metadata is used to implement cross-cutting concerns based on policies and configuration attached to each endpoint.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d429d-269">L’intergiciel (middleware) terminal peut être un outil efficace, mais peut nécessiter les éléments suivants :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-269">Terminal middleware can be an effective tool, but can require:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="d429d-270">Une quantité significative de codage et de test.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-270">A significant amount of coding and testing.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="d429d-271">Intégration manuelle avec d’autres systèmes pour atteindre le niveau de flexibilité souhaité.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-271">Manual integration with other systems to achieve the desired level of flexibility.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d429d-272">Envisagez l’intégration avec le routage avant d’écrire un intergiciel (middleware) Terminal.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-272">Consider integrating with routing before writing a terminal middleware.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d429d-273">Un intergiciel (middleware) terminal existant qui s’intègre à [Map](xref:fundamentals/middleware/index#branch-the-middleware-pipeline) ou <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapWhenExtensions.MapWhen*> peut généralement être converti en point de terminaison prenant en charge le routage.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-273">Existing terminal middleware that integrates with [Map](xref:fundamentals/middleware/index#branch-the-middleware-pipeline) or <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.MapWhenExtensions.MapWhen*> can usually be turned into a routing aware endpoint.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-274">[MapHealthChecks](https://github.com/aspnet/AspNetCore/blob/master/src/Middleware/HealthChecks/src/Builder/HealthCheckEndpointRouteBuilderExtensions.cs#L16) illustre le modèle de routeur-Ware :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-274">[MapHealthChecks](https://github.com/aspnet/AspNetCore/blob/master/src/Middleware/HealthChecks/src/Builder/HealthCheckEndpointRouteBuilderExtensions.cs#L16) demonstrates the pattern for router-ware:</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="d429d-275">Écrire une méthode d’extension sur <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IEndpointRouteBuilder> .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-275">Write an extension method on <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IEndpointRouteBuilder>.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="d429d-276">Créez un pipeline d’intergiciel (middleware) imbriqué à l’aide de <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IEndpointRouteBuilder.CreateApplicationBuilder*> .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-276">Create a nested middleware pipeline using <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IEndpointRouteBuilder.CreateApplicationBuilder*>.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="d429d-277">Attachez l’intergiciel au nouveau pipeline.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-277">Attach the middleware to the new pipeline.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-278">Dans ce cas, <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.HealthCheckApplicationBuilderExtensions.UseHealthChecks*>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-278">In this case, <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.HealthCheckApplicationBuilderExtensions.UseHealthChecks*>.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="d429d-279"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.IApplicationBuilder.Build*>pipeline d’intergiciel (middleware) dans un <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.RequestDelegate> .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-279"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.IApplicationBuilder.Build*> the middleware pipeline into a <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Http.RequestDelegate>.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="d429d-280">Appelez `Map` et fournissez le nouveau pipeline d’intergiciel (middleware).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-280">Call `Map` and provide the new middleware pipeline.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="d429d-281">Retourne l’objet générateur fourni par `Map` à partir de la méthode d’extension.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-281">Return the builder object provided by `Map` from the extension method.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d429d-282">Le code suivant illustre l’utilisation de [MapHealthChecks](xref:host-and-deploy/health-checks):</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-282">The following code shows use of [MapHealthChecks](xref:host-and-deploy/health-checks):</span></span>
