## <a name="use-routing-middleware"></a><span data-ttu-id="d429d-1074">Utilisation du middleware de routage</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1074">Use Routing Middleware</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d429d-1075">Référencez le [métapackage Microsoft.AspNetCore.App](xref:fundamentals/metapackage-app) dans le fichier projet de l’application.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1075">Reference the [Microsoft.AspNetCore.App metapackage](xref:fundamentals/metapackage-app) in the app's project file.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d429d-1076">Ajoutez le routage au conteneur de service dans `Startup.ConfigureServices` :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1076">Add routing to the service container in `Startup.ConfigureServices`:</span></span>

[!code-csharp[](routing/samples/2.x/RoutingSample/Startup.cs?name=snippet_ConfigureServices&highlight=3)]

<span data-ttu-id="d429d-1077">Les routes doivent être configurées dans la méthode `Startup.Configure`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1077">Routes must be configured in the `Startup.Configure` method.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1078">L’exemple d’application utilise les API suivantes :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1078">The sample app uses the following APIs:</span></span>

* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteBuilder>
* <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1079"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapGet*>: Correspond uniquement aux requêtes HTTP.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1079"><xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapGet*>: Matches only HTTP GET requests.</span></span>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Builder.RoutingBuilderExtensions.UseRouter*>

[!code-csharp[](routing/samples/2.x/RoutingSample/Startup.cs?name=snippet_RouteHandler)]

<span data-ttu-id="d429d-1080">Le tableau suivant montre les réponses avec les URI donnés.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1080">The following table shows the responses with the given URIs.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1081">URI</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1081">URI</span></span>                    | <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1082">response</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1082">Response</span></span>                                          |
| ---------------------- | ------------------------------------------------- |
| `/package/create/3`    | <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1083">Hello!</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1083">Hello!</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1084">Valeurs de route : [operation, create], [id, 3]</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1084">Route values: [operation, create], [id, 3]</span></span> |
| `/package/track/-3`    | <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1085">Hello!</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1085">Hello!</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1086">Valeurs de route : [operation, track], [id, -3]</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1086">Route values: [operation, track], [id, -3]</span></span> |
| `/package/track/-3/`   | <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1087">Hello!</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1087">Hello!</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1088">Valeurs de route : [operation, track], [id, -3]</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1088">Route values: [operation, track], [id, -3]</span></span> |
| `/package/track/`      | <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1089">La requête passe à travers ceci, aucune correspondance.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1089">The request falls through, no match.</span></span>              |
| `GET /hello/Joe`       | <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1090">Hi, Joe!</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1090">Hi, Joe!</span></span>                                          |
| `POST /hello/Joe`      | <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1091">La requête passe à travers ceci, correspondance seulement avec HTTP GET.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1091">The request falls through, matches HTTP GET only.</span></span> |
| `GET /hello/Joe/Smith` | <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1092">La requête passe à travers ceci, aucune correspondance.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1092">The request falls through, no match.</span></span>              |

<span data-ttu-id="d429d-1093">Le framework fournit un ensemble de méthodes d’extension pour la création de routes (<xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions>) :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1093">The framework provides a set of extension methods for creating routes (<xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions>):</span></span>

* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapDelete*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapGet*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapMiddlewareDelete*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapMiddlewareGet*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapMiddlewarePost*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapMiddlewarePut*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapMiddlewareRoute*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapMiddlewareVerb*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapPost*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapPut*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapRoute*>
* <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapVerb*>

<span data-ttu-id="d429d-1094">Les méthodes `Map[Verb]` utilisent des contraintes pour limiter la route au verbe HTTP dans le nom de la méthode.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1094">The `Map[Verb]` methods use constraints to limit the route to the HTTP Verb in the method name.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1095">Par exemple, consultez <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapGet*> et <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapVerb*>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1095">For example, see <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapGet*> and <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RequestDelegateRouteBuilderExtensions.MapVerb*>.</span></span>

## <a name="route-template-reference"></a><span data-ttu-id="d429d-1096">Informations de référence sur les modèles de routage</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1096">Route template reference</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d429d-1097">Les jetons placés entre accolades (`{ ... }`) définissent des *paramètres de routage* qui sont liés si une correspondance est trouvée pour la route.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1097">Tokens within curly braces (`{ ... }`) define *route parameters* that are bound if the route is matched.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1098">Vous pouvez définir plusieurs paramètres de routage dans un segment de route, mais ils doivent être séparés par une valeur littérale.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1098">You can define more than one route parameter in a route segment, but they must be separated by a literal value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1099">Par exemple `{controller=Home}{action=Index}` n’est pas une route valide, car il n’y a aucune valeur littérale entre `{controller}` et `{action}`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1099">For example, `{controller=Home}{action=Index}` isn't a valid route, since there's no literal value between `{controller}` and `{action}`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1100">Ces paramètres de routage doivent avoir un nom, et ils autorisent la spécification d’attributs supplémentaires.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1100">These route parameters must have a name and may have additional attributes specified.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d429d-1101">Un texte littéral autre que les paramètres de routage (par exemple, `{id}`) et le séparateur de chemin `/` doit correspondre au texte présent dans l’URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1101">Literal text other than route parameters (for example, `{id}`) and the path separator `/` must match the text in the URL.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1102">La correspondance de texte ne respecte pas la casse et est basée sur la représentation décodée du chemin des URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1102">Text matching is case-insensitive and based on the decoded representation of the URLs path.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1103">Pour mettre en correspondance un délimiteur de paramètre de route littéral (`{` ou `}`), placez-le dans une séquence d’échappement en répétant le caractère (`{{` ou `}}`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1103">To match a literal route parameter delimiter (`{` or `}`), escape the delimiter by repeating the character (`{{` or `}}`).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d429d-1104">Les modèles d’URL qui tentent de capturer un nom de fichier avec une extension de fichier facultative doivent faire l’objet de considérations supplémentaires.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1104">URL patterns that attempt to capture a file name with an optional file extension have additional considerations.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1105">Prenez par exemple le modèle `files/{filename}.{ext?}`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1105">For example, consider the template `files/{filename}.{ext?}`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1106">Quand des valeurs existent à la fois pour `filename` et pour `ext`, les deux valeurs sont renseignées.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1106">When values for both `filename` and `ext` exist, both values are populated.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1107">Si seule une valeur existe pour `filename` dans l’URL, une correspondance est trouvée pour la route, car le point final (`.`) est facultatif.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1107">If only a value for `filename` exists in the URL, the route matches because the trailing period (`.`) is  optional.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1108">Les URL suivantes correspondent à cette route :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1108">The following URLs match this route:</span></span>

* `/files/myFile.txt`
* `/files/myFile`

<span data-ttu-id="d429d-1109">Vous pouvez utiliser un astérisque (`*`) ou un double astérisque (`**`) comme préfixe d’un paramètre de route à lier au reste de l’URI.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1109">You can use an asterisk (`*`) or double asterisk (`**`) as a prefix to a route parameter to bind to the rest of the URI.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1110">Ils sont appelés des paramètres *passe-partout*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1110">These are called a *catch-all* parameters.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1111">Par exemple, `blog/{**slug}` établit une correspondance avec n’importe quel URI commençant par `/blog` et suivi de n’importe quelle valeur, qui est affectée à la valeur de route `slug`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1111">For example, `blog/{**slug}` matches any URI that starts with `/blog` and has any value following it, which is assigned to the `slug` route value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1112">Les paramètres fourre-tout peuvent également établir une correspondance avec la chaîne vide.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1112">Catch-all parameters can also match the empty string.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d429d-1113">Le paramètre fourre-tout place les caractères appropriés dans une séquence d’échappement lorsque la route est utilisée pour générer une URL, y compris les caractères de séparation de chemin (`/`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1113">The catch-all parameter escapes the appropriate characters when the route is used to generate a URL, including path separator (`/`) characters.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1114">Par exemple, la route `foo/{*path}` avec les valeurs de route `{ path = "my/path" }` génère `foo/my%2Fpath`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1114">For example, the route `foo/{*path}` with route values `{ path = "my/path" }` generates `foo/my%2Fpath`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1115">Notez la barre oblique d’échappement.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1115">Note the escaped forward slash.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1116">Pour les séparateurs de chemin aller-retour, utilisez le préfixe de paramètre de routage `**`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1116">To round-trip path separator characters, use the `**` route parameter prefix.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1117">La route `foo/{**path}` avec `{ path = "my/path" }` génère `foo/my/path`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1117">The route `foo/{**path}` with `{ path = "my/path" }` generates `foo/my/path`.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d429d-1118">Les paramètres de route peuvent avoir des *valeurs par défaut*, désignées en spécifiant la valeur par défaut après le nom du paramètre, séparée par un signe égal (`=`).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1118">Route parameters may have *default values* designated by specifying the default value after the parameter name separated by an equals sign (`=`).</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1119">Par exemple, `{controller=Home}` définit `Home` comme valeur par défaut de `controller`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1119">For example, `{controller=Home}` defines `Home` as the default value for `controller`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1120">La valeur par défaut est utilisée si aucune valeur n’est présente dans l’URL pour le paramètre.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1120">The default value is used if no value is present in the URL for the parameter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1121">Vous pouvez rendre facultatifs les paramètres de route en ajoutant un point d’interrogation (`?`) à la fin du nom du paramètre, comme dans `id?`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1121">Route parameters are made optional by appending a question mark (`?`) to the end of the parameter name, as in `id?`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1122">La différence entre les valeurs facultatives et les paramètres de route par défaut est qu’un paramètre de route ayant une valeur par défaut produit toujours une valeur, tandis qu’un paramètre facultatif a une valeur seulement quand celle-ci est fournie par l’URL de requête.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1122">The difference between optional values and default route parameters is that a route parameter with a default value always produces a value&mdash;an optional parameter has a value only when a value is provided by the request URL.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d429d-1123">Les paramètres de route peuvent avoir des contraintes, qui doivent correspondre à la valeur de route liée à partir de l’URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1123">Route parameters may have constraints that must match the route value bound from the URL.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1124">L’ajout d’un signe deux-points (`:`) et d’un nom de contrainte après le nom du paramètre de routage spécifie une *contrainte inline* sur un paramètre de routage.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1124">Adding a colon (`:`) and constraint name after the route parameter name specifies an *inline constraint* on a route parameter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1125">Si la contrainte nécessite des arguments, ils sont fournis entre parenthèses (`(...)`) après le nom de la contrainte.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1125">If the constraint requires arguments, they're enclosed in parentheses (`(...)`) after the constraint name.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1126">Il est possible de spécifier plusieurs contraintes inline en ajoutant un autre signe deux-points (`:`) et le nom d’une autre contrainte.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1126">Multiple inline constraints can be specified by appending another colon (`:`) and constraint name.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d429d-1127">Le nom de la contrainte et les arguments sont passés au service <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IInlineConstraintResolver> pour créer une instance de <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> à utiliser dans le traitement des URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1127">The constraint name and arguments are passed to the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IInlineConstraintResolver> service to create an instance of <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> to use in URL processing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1128">Par exemple, le modèle de routage `blog/{article:minlength(10)}` spécifie une contrainte `minlength` avec l’argument `10`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1128">For example, the route template `blog/{article:minlength(10)}` specifies a `minlength` constraint with the argument `10`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1129">Pour plus d’informations sur les contraintes de route et pour obtenir la liste des contraintes fournies par le framework, consultez la section [Informations de référence sur les contraintes de route](#route-constraint-reference).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1129">For more information on route constraints and a list of the constraints provided by the framework, see the [Route constraint reference](#route-constraint-reference) section.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d429d-1130">Les paramètres de route peuvent également contenir des transformateurs de paramètre, qui transforment une valeur de paramètre lors de la génération des liens et de la mise en correspondance des actions et des pages avec les URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1130">Route parameters may also have parameter transformers, which transform a parameter's value when generating links and matching actions and pages to URLs.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1131">À l’instar des contraintes, les transformateurs de paramètre peuvent être ajoutés inline à un paramètre de routage en ajoutant un signe deux-points (`:`) et le nom du transformateur après le nom du paramètre de routage.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1131">Like constraints, parameter transformers can be added inline to a route parameter by adding a colon (`:`) and transformer name after the route parameter name.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1132">Par exemple, le modèle de routage `blog/{article:slugify}` spécifie un transformateur `slugify`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1132">For example, the route template `blog/{article:slugify}` specifies a `slugify` transformer.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1133">Pour plus d’informations sur les transformateurs de paramètre, consultez la section [Informations de référence sur les transformateurs de paramètre](#parameter-transformer-reference).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1133">For more information on parameter transformers, see the [Parameter transformer reference](#parameter-transformer-reference) section.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d429d-1134">Le tableau suivant montre des exemples de modèles de route et leur comportement.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1134">The following table demonstrates example route templates and their behavior.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1135">Modèle de routage</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1135">Route Template</span></span>                           | <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1136">Exemple d’URI en correspondance</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1136">Example Matching URI</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1137">URI de la requête&hellip;</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1137">The request URI&hellip;</span></span>                                                    |
| ---------------------------------------- | ----------------------- | -------------------------------------------------------------------------- |
| `hello`                                  | `/hello`                | <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1138">Correspond seulement au chemin unique `/hello`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1138">Only matches the single path `/hello`.</span></span>                                     |
| `{Page=Home}`                            | `/`                     | <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1139">Correspond à `Page` et le définit sur `Home`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1139">Matches and sets `Page` to `Home`.</span></span>                                         |
| `{Page=Home}`                            | `/Contact`              | <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1140">Correspond à `Page` et le définit sur `Contact`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1140">Matches and sets `Page` to `Contact`.</span></span>                                      |
| `{controller}/{action}/{id?}`            | `/Products/List`        | <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1141">Mappe au contrôleur `Products` et à l’action `List`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1141">Maps to the `Products` controller and `List` action.</span></span>                       |
| `{controller}/{action}/{id?}`            | `/Products/Details/123` | <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1142">Mappe au contrôleur `Products` et à l’action `Details` (`id` défini sur 123).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1142">Maps to the `Products` controller and  `Details` action (`id` set to 123).</span></span> |
| `{controller=Home}/{action=Index}/{id?}` | `/`                     | <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1143">Mappe au contrôleur `Home` et à la méthode `Index` (`id` est ignoré).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1143">Maps to the `Home` controller and `Index` method (`id` is ignored).</span></span>        |

<span data-ttu-id="d429d-1144">L’utilisation d’un modèle est généralement l’approche la plus simple pour le routage.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1144">Using a template is generally the simplest approach to routing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1145">Il est également possible de spécifier des contraintes et des valeurs par défaut hors du modèle de routage.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1145">Constraints and defaults can also be specified outside the route template.</span></span>

> [!TIP]
> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1146">Activez la [journalisation](xref:fundamentals/logging/index) pour voir comment les implémentations de routage intégrées, comme <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route>, établissent des correspondances avec les requêtes.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1146">Enable [Logging](xref:fundamentals/logging/index) to see how the built-in routing implementations, such as <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route>, match requests.</span></span>

## <a name="reserved-routing-names"></a><span data-ttu-id="d429d-1147">Noms de routage réservés</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1147">Reserved routing names</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d429d-1148">Les mots clés suivants sont des noms réservés qui ne peuvent pas être utilisés comme paramètres ou noms de routage :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1148">The following keywords are reserved names and can't be used as route names or parameters:</span></span>

* `action`
* `area`
* `controller`
* `handler`
* `page`

## <a name="route-constraint-reference"></a><span data-ttu-id="d429d-1149">Informations de référence sur les contraintes de routage</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1149">Route constraint reference</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d429d-1150">Les contraintes de route s’exécutent quand une correspondance s’est produite pour l’URL entrante, et le chemin de l’URL est tokenisé en valeurs de route.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1150">Route constraints execute when a match has occurred to the incoming URL and the URL path is tokenized into route values.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1151">En général, les contraintes de routage inspectent la valeur de route associée par le biais du modèle de routage, et créent une décision oui/non indiquant si la valeur est, ou non, acceptable.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1151">Route constraints generally inspect the route value associated via the route template and make a yes/no decision about whether or not the value is acceptable.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1152">Certaines contraintes de routage utilisent des données hors de la valeur de route pour déterminer si la requête peut être routée.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1152">Some route constraints use data outside the route value to consider whether the request can be routed.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1153">Par exemple, <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Constraints.HttpMethodRouteConstraint> peut accepter ou rejeter une requête en fonction de son verbe HTTP.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1153">For example, the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Constraints.HttpMethodRouteConstraint> can accept or reject a request based on its HTTP verb.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1154">Les contraintes sont utilisées dans le routage des requêtes et la génération des liens.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1154">Constraints are used in routing requests and link generation.</span></span>

> [!WARNING]
> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1155">N’utilisez pas de contraintes pour la **validation des entrées**.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1155">Don't use constraints for **input validation**.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1156">Si des contraintes sont utilisées pour la **validation des entrées**, une entrée non valide génère une réponse *404 - Introuvable* au lieu d’une réponse *400 - Requête incorrecte* avec un message d’erreur approprié.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1156">If constraints are used for **input validation**, invalid input results in a *404 - Not Found* response instead of a *400 - Bad Request* with an appropriate error message.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1157">Les contraintes de route sont utilisées pour **lever l’ambiguïté** entre des routes similaires, et non pas pour valider les entrées d’une route particulière.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1157">Route constraints are used to **disambiguate** similar routes, not to validate the inputs for a particular route.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d429d-1158">Le tableau suivant montre des exemples de contrainte de route et leur comportement attendu.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1158">The following table demonstrates example route constraints and their expected behavior.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1159">Contrainte</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1159">Constraint</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1160">Exemple</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1160">Example</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1161">Exemples de correspondances</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1161">Example matches</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1162">Notes</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1162">Notes</span></span> |
|------------|---------|-----------------|-------|
| `int` | `{id:int}` | <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1163">`123456789`, `-123456789`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1163">`123456789`, `-123456789`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1164">Correspond à n’importe quel entier.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1164">Matches any integer.</span></span>|
| `bool` | `{active:bool}` | <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1165">`true`, `FALSE`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1165">`true`, `FALSE`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1166">Correspond à `true` ou `false` .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1166">Matches `true` or `false`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1167">Non-respect de la casse.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1167">Case-insensitive.</span></span>|
| `datetime` | `{dob:datetime}` | <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1168">`2016-12-31`, `2016-12-31 7:32pm`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1168">`2016-12-31`, `2016-12-31 7:32pm`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1169">Correspond à une `DateTime` valeur valide dans la culture dite indifférente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1169">Matches a valid `DateTime` value in the invariant culture.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1170">Consultez l’avertissement précédent.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1170">See preceding warning.</span></span>|
| `decimal` | `{price:decimal}` | <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1171">`49.99`, `-1,000.01`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1171">`49.99`, `-1,000.01`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1172">Correspond à une `decimal` valeur valide dans la culture dite indifférente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1172">Matches a valid `decimal` value in the invariant culture.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1173">Consultez l’avertissement précédent.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1173">See  preceding warning.</span></span>|
| `double` | `{weight:double}` | <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1174">`1.234`, `-1,001.01e8`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1174">`1.234`, `-1,001.01e8`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1175">Correspond à une `double` valeur valide dans la culture dite indifférente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1175">Matches a valid `double` value in the invariant culture.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1176">Consultez l’avertissement précédent.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1176">See  preceding warning.</span></span>|
| `float` | `{weight:float}` | <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1177">`1.234`, `-1,001.01e8`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1177">`1.234`, `-1,001.01e8`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1178">Correspond à une `float` valeur valide dans la culture dite indifférente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1178">Matches a valid `float` value in the invariant culture.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1179">Consultez l’avertissement précédent.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1179">See  preceding warning.</span></span>|
| `guid` | `{id:guid}` | <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1180">`CD2C1638-1638-72D5-1638-DEADBEEF1638`, `{CD2C1638-1638-72D5-1638-DEADBEEF1638}`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1180">`CD2C1638-1638-72D5-1638-DEADBEEF1638`, `{CD2C1638-1638-72D5-1638-DEADBEEF1638}`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1181">Correspond à une `Guid` valeur valide.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1181">Matches a valid `Guid` value.</span></span>|
| `long` | `{ticks:long}` | <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1182">`123456789`, `-123456789`</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1182">`123456789`, `-123456789`</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1183">Correspond à une `long` valeur valide.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1183">Matches a valid `long` value.</span></span>|
| `minlength(value)` | `{username:minlength(4)}` | `Rick` | <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1184">La chaîne doit comporter au moins 4 caractères.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1184">String must be at least 4 characters.</span></span>|
| `maxlength(value)` | `{filename:maxlength(8)}` | `MyFile` | <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1185">La chaîne ne doit pas comporter plus de 8 caractères.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1185">String has maximum of 8 characters.</span></span>|
| `length(length)` | `{filename:length(12)}` | `somefile.txt` | <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1186">La chaîne doit contenir exactement 12 caractères.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1186">String must be exactly 12 characters long.</span></span>|
| `length(min,max)` | `{filename:length(8,16)}` | `somefile.txt` | <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1187">La chaîne doit être au moins égale à 8 et comporter jusqu’à 16 caractères.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1187">String must be at least 8 and has maximum of 16 characters.</span></span>|
| `min(value)` | `{age:min(18)}` | `19` | <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1188">La valeur entière doit être au moins égale à 18.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1188">Integer value must be at least 18.</span></span>|
| `max(value)` | `{age:max(120)}` | `91` | <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1189">Valeur entière maximale de 120.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1189">Integer value maximum of 120.</span></span>|
| `range(min,max)` | `{age:range(18,120)}` | `91` | <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1190">La valeur entière doit être au moins égale à 18 et 120.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1190">Integer value must be at least 18 and maximum of 120.</span></span>|
| `alpha` | `{name:alpha}` | `Rick` | <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1191">La chaîne doit comporter un ou plusieurs caractères alphabétiques `a` - `z` .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1191">String must consist of one or more alphabetical characters `a`-`z`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1192">Non-respect de la casse.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1192">Case-insensitive.</span></span>|
| `regex(expression)` | `{ssn:regex(^\\d{{3}}-\\d{{2}}-\\d{{4}}$)}` | `123-45-6789` | <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1193">La chaîne doit correspondre à l’expression régulière.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1193">String must match the regular expression.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1194">Consultez les conseils relatifs à la définition d’une expression régulière.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1194">See tips about defining a regular expression.</span></span>|
| `required` | `{name:required}` | `Rick` | <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1195">Permet d’appliquer qu’une valeur sans paramètre est présente pendant la génération de l’URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1195">Used to enforce that a non-parameter value is present during URL generation.</span></span>|

<span data-ttu-id="d429d-1196">Il est possible d’appliquer plusieurs contraintes séparées par un point-virgule à un même paramètre.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1196">Multiple, colon-delimited constraints can be applied to a single parameter.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1197">Par exemple, la contrainte suivante limite un paramètre à une valeur entière supérieure ou égale à 1 :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1197">For example, the following constraint restricts a parameter to an integer value of 1 or greater:</span></span>

```csharp
[Route("users/{id:int:min(1)}")]
public User GetUserById(int id) { }
```

> [!WARNING]
> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1198">Les contraintes de routage qui vérifient que l’URL peut être convertie en type CLR (comme `int` ou `DateTime`) utilisent toujours la culture invariant.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1198">Route constraints that verify the URL and are converted to a CLR type (such as `int` or `DateTime`) always use the invariant culture.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1199">ces contraintes partent du principe que l’URL n’est pas localisable.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1199">These constraints assume that the URL is non-localizable.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1200">Les contraintes de routage fournies par le framework ne modifient pas les valeurs stockées dans les valeurs de route.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1200">The framework-provided route constraints don't modify the values stored in route values.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1201">Toutes les valeurs de route analysées à partir de l’URL sont stockées sous forme de chaînes.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1201">All route values parsed from the URL are stored as strings.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1202">Par exemple, la contrainte `float` tente de convertir la valeur de route en valeur float, mais la valeur convertie est utilisée uniquement pour vérifier qu’elle peut être convertie en valeur float.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1202">For example, the `float` constraint attempts to convert the route value to a float, but the converted value is used only to verify it can be converted to a float.</span></span>

## <a name="regular-expressions"></a><span data-ttu-id="d429d-1203">Expressions régulières</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1203">Regular expressions</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d429d-1204">Le framework ASP.NET Core ajoute `RegexOptions.IgnoreCase | RegexOptions.Compiled | RegexOptions.CultureInvariant` au constructeur d’expression régulière.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1204">The ASP.NET Core framework adds `RegexOptions.IgnoreCase | RegexOptions.Compiled | RegexOptions.CultureInvariant` to the regular expression constructor.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1205">Pour obtenir une description de ces membres, consultez <xref:System.Text.RegularExpressions.RegexOptions>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1205">See <xref:System.Text.RegularExpressions.RegexOptions> for a description of these members.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d429d-1206">Les expressions régulières utilisent des délimiteurs et des jetons similaires à ceux utilisés par le routage et le langage C#.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1206">Regular expressions use delimiters and tokens similar to those used by routing and the C# language.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1207">Les jetons d’expression régulière doivent être placés dans une séquence d’échappement.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1207">Regular expression tokens must be escaped.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1208">Pour utiliser l’expression régulière `^\d{3}-\d{2}-\d{4}$` dans le routage :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1208">To use the regular expression `^\d{3}-\d{2}-\d{4}$` in routing:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1209">L’expression doit avoir les caractères de barre oblique inverse uniques `\` fournis dans la chaîne sous la forme de caractères barre oblique inverse doubles `\\` dans le code source.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1209">The expression must have the single backslash `\` characters provided in the string as double backslash `\\` characters in the source code.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1210">L’expression régulière doit nous permettre d' `\\` échapper le caractère d’échappement de la `\` chaîne.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1210">The regular expression must us `\\` in order to escape the `\` string escape character.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1211">L’expression régulière n’est pas nécessaire `\\` lors de l’utilisation de [littéraux de chaîne Verbatim](/dotnet/csharp/language-reference/keywords/string).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1211">The regular expression doesn't require `\\` when using [verbatim string literals](/dotnet/csharp/language-reference/keywords/string).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d429d-1212">Pour échapper les caractères de délimiteur de paramètre de routage `{` , `}` ,, `[` `]` , doublez les caractères dans l’expression `{{` , `}` `[[` `]]` ,,.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1212">To escape routing parameter delimiter characters `{`, `}`, `[`, `]`, double the characters in the expression `{{`, `}`, `[[`, `]]`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1213">Le tableau suivant montre une expression régulière et la version échappée :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1213">The following table shows a regular expression and the escaped version:</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1214">Expression régulière</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1214">Regular Expression</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1215">Expression régulière en échappement</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1215">Escaped Regular Expression</span></span>     |
| --------------------- | ------------------------------ |
| `^\d{3}-\d{2}-\d{4}$` | `^\\d{{3}}-\\d{{2}}-\\d{{4}}$` |
| `^[a-z]{2}$`          | `^[[a-z]]{{2}}$`               |

<span data-ttu-id="d429d-1216">Les expressions régulières utilisées dans le routage commencent souvent par le `^` caractère de signe insertion et correspondent à la position de départ de la chaîne.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1216">Regular expressions used in routing often start with the caret `^` character and match starting position of the string.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1217">Les expressions se terminent souvent par le `$` caractère de signe dollar et la fin de la chaîne.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1217">The expressions often end with the dollar sign `$` character and match end of the string.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1218">Les caractères `^` et `$` garantissent que l’expression régulière établit une correspondance avec la totalité de la valeur du paramètre de route.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1218">The `^` and `$` characters ensure that the regular expression match the entire route parameter value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1219">Sans les caractères `^` et `$`, l’expression régulière peut correspondre à n’importe quelle sous-chaîne dans la chaîne, ce qui est souvent indésirable.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1219">Without the `^` and `$` characters, the regular expression match any substring within the string, which is often undesirable.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1220">Le tableau suivant contient des exemples et explique pourquoi ils établissent ou non une correspondance.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1220">The following table provides examples and explains why they match or fail to match.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1221">Expression</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1221">Expression</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1222">String</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1222">String</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1223">Faire correspondre</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1223">Match</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1224">Commentaire</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1224">Comment</span></span>               |
| ------------ | --------- | :---: |  -------------------- |
| `[a-z]{2}`   | <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1225">hello</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1225">hello</span></span>     | <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1226">Oui</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1226">Yes</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1227">Correspondances de sous-chaînes</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1227">Substring matches</span></span>     |
| `[a-z]{2}`   | <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1228">123abc456</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1228">123abc456</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1229">Oui</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1229">Yes</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1230">Correspondances de sous-chaînes</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1230">Substring matches</span></span>     |
| `[a-z]{2}`   | <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1231">mz</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1231">mz</span></span>        | <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1232">Oui</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1232">Yes</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1233">Correspondance avec l’expression</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1233">Matches expression</span></span>    |
| `[a-z]{2}`   | <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1234">MZ</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1234">MZ</span></span>        | <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1235">Oui</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1235">Yes</span></span>   | <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1236">Non-respect de la casse</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1236">Not case sensitive</span></span>    |
| `^[a-z]{2}$` | <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1237">hello</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1237">hello</span></span>     | <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1238">Non</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1238">No</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1239">Voir `^` et `$` ci-dessus</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1239">See `^` and `$` above</span></span> |
| `^[a-z]{2}$` | <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1240">123abc456</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1240">123abc456</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1241">Non</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1241">No</span></span>    | <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1242">Voir `^` et `$` ci-dessus</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1242">See `^` and `$` above</span></span> |

<span data-ttu-id="d429d-1243">Pour plus d’informations sur la syntaxe des expressions régulières, consultez [Expressions régulières du .NET Framework](/dotnet/standard/base-types/regular-expression-language-quick-reference).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1243">For more information on regular expression syntax, see [.NET Framework Regular Expressions](/dotnet/standard/base-types/regular-expression-language-quick-reference).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d429d-1244">Pour contraindre un paramètre à un ensemble connu de valeurs possibles, utilisez une expression régulière.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1244">To constrain a parameter to a known set of possible values, use a regular expression.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1245">Par exemple, `{action:regex(^(list|get|create)$)}` établit une correspondance avec la valeur de route `action` uniquement pour `list`, `get` ou `create`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1245">For example, `{action:regex(^(list|get|create)$)}` only matches the `action` route value to `list`, `get`, or `create`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1246">Si elle est passée dans le dictionnaire de contraintes, la chaîne `^(list|get|create)$` est équivalente.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1246">If passed into the constraints dictionary, the string `^(list|get|create)$` is equivalent.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1247">Les contraintes passées dans le dictionnaire de contraintes (c’est-à-dire qui ne sont pas inline dans un modèle) qui ne correspondent pas à l’une des contraintes connues sont également traitées comme des expressions régulières.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1247">Constraints that are passed in the constraints dictionary (not inline within a template) that don't match one of the known constraints are also treated as regular expressions.</span></span>

## <a name="custom-route-constraints"></a><span data-ttu-id="d429d-1248">Contraintes d’itinéraire personnalisées</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1248">Custom route constraints</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d429d-1249">Outre les contraintes d’itinéraire intégré, les contraintes d’itinéraire personnalisé peuvent être créées en implémentant l’interface <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1249">In addition to the built-in route constraints, custom route constraints can be created by implementing the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> interface.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1250">L’interface <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> contient une méthode unique, `Match`, qui retourne `true` si la contrainte est satisfaite et `false` dans le cas contraire.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1250">The <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> interface contains a single method, `Match`, which returns `true` if the constraint is satisfied and `false` otherwise.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d429d-1251">Pour utiliser un <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> personnalisé, le type de contrainte d’itinéraire doit être inscrit avec le <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> de l’application dans le conteneur de service de l’application.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1251">To use a custom <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint>, the route constraint type must be registered with the app's <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> in the app's service container.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1252">Un <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> est un dictionnaire qui mappe les clés de contrainte d’itinéraire aux implémentations <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> qui valident ces contraintes.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1252">A <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> is a dictionary that maps route constraint keys to <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IRouteConstraint> implementations that validate those constraints.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1253">Le <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> d’une application peut être mis à jour dans `Startup.ConfigureServices` dans le cadre d’un appel [services.AddRouting](xref:Microsoft.Extensions.DependencyInjection.RoutingServiceCollectionExtensions.AddRouting*) ou en configurant <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions> directement avec `services.Configure<RouteOptions>`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1253">An app's <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> can be updated in `Startup.ConfigureServices` either as part of a [services.AddRouting](xref:Microsoft.Extensions.DependencyInjection.RoutingServiceCollectionExtensions.AddRouting*) call or by configuring <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions> directly with `services.Configure<RouteOptions>`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1254">Par exemple :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1254">For example:</span></span>

```csharp
services.AddRouting(options =>
{
    options.ConstraintMap.Add("customName", typeof(MyCustomConstraint));
});
```

<span data-ttu-id="d429d-1255">La contrainte peut ensuite être appliquée aux itinéraires de la manière habituelle, en utilisant le nom spécifié lors de l’inscription du type de contrainte.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1255">The constraint can then be applied to routes in the usual manner, using the name specified when registering the constraint type.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1256">Par exemple :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1256">For example:</span></span>

```csharp
[HttpGet("{id:customName}")]
public ActionResult<string> Get(string id)
```

## <a name="parameter-transformer-reference"></a><span data-ttu-id="d429d-1257">Informations de référence sur le transformateur de paramètre</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1257">Parameter transformer reference</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d429d-1258">Transformateurs de paramètre :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1258">Parameter transformers:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1259">Sont exécutés lors de la génération d’un lien pour un <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1259">Execute when generating a link for a <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.Route>.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1260">Implémentez `Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IOutboundParameterTransformer`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1260">Implement `Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.IOutboundParameterTransformer`.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1261">Sont configurés à l’aide de <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1261">Are configured using <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap>.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1262">Prennent la valeur de routage du paramètre et la convertissent en une nouvelle valeur de chaîne.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1262">Take the parameter's route value and transform it to a new string value.</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1263">Aboutissent à l’utilisation de la valeur transformée dans le lien généré.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1263">Result in using the transformed value in the generated link.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d429d-1264">Par exemple, un transformateur de paramètre `slugify` personnalisé dans le modèle d’itinéraire `blog\{article:slugify}` avec `Url.Action(new { article = "MyTestArticle" })` génère `blog\my-test-article`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1264">For example, a custom `slugify` parameter transformer in route pattern `blog\{article:slugify}` with `Url.Action(new { article = "MyTestArticle" })` generates `blog\my-test-article`.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d429d-1265">Pour utiliser un transformateur de paramètre dans un modèle d’itinéraire, configurez-le d’abord en utilisant <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> dans `Startup.ConfigureServices` :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1265">To use a parameter transformer in a route pattern, configure it first using <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteOptions.ConstraintMap> in `Startup.ConfigureServices`:</span></span>

```csharp
services.AddRouting(options =>
{
    // Replace the type and the name used to refer to it with your own
    // IOutboundParameterTransformer implementation
    options.ConstraintMap["slugify"] = typeof(SlugifyParameterTransformer);
});
```

<span data-ttu-id="d429d-1266">Les transformateurs de paramètre sont utilisés par le framework pour transformer l’URI où un point de terminaison est résolu.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1266">Parameter transformers are used by the framework to transform the URI where an endpoint resolves.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1267">Par exemple, ASP.NET Core MVC utilise des transformateurs de paramètre pour convertir la valeur de routage utilisée et la faire correspondre à un `area`, `controller`, `action` et `page`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1267">For example, ASP.NET Core MVC uses parameter transformers to transform the route value used to match an `area`, `controller`, `action`, and `page`.</span></span>

```csharp
routes.MapRoute(
    name: "default",
    template: "{controller:slugify=Home}/{action:slugify=Index}/{id?}");
```

<span data-ttu-id="d429d-1268">Avec la route précédente, l’action `SubscriptionManagementController.GetAll` est mise en correspondance avec l’URI `/subscription-management/get-all`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1268">With the preceding route, the action `SubscriptionManagementController.GetAll` is matched with the URI `/subscription-management/get-all`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1269">Un transformateur de paramètre ne modifie pas les valeurs de routage utilisées pour générer un lien.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1269">A parameter transformer doesn't change the route values used to generate a link.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1270">Par exemple, `Url.Action("GetAll", "SubscriptionManagement")` produit `/subscription-management/get-all`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1270">For example, `Url.Action("GetAll", "SubscriptionManagement")` outputs `/subscription-management/get-all`.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d429d-1271">ASP.NET Core fournit des conventions d’API pour l’utilisation des transformateurs de paramètre avec des routages générés :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1271">ASP.NET Core provides API conventions for using a parameter transformers with generated routes:</span></span>

* <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1272">La convention de l’API `Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.ApplicationModels.RouteTokenTransformerConvention` est fournie avec ASP.NET Core MVC.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1272">ASP.NET Core MVC has the `Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.ApplicationModels.RouteTokenTransformerConvention` API convention.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1273">Cette convention applique un transformateur de paramètre spécifié à tous les routages d’attributs dans l’application.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1273">This convention applies a specified parameter transformer to all attribute routes in the app.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1274">Le transformateur de paramètre transforme les jetons de routage d’attribut quand ils sont remplacés.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1274">The parameter transformer transforms attribute route tokens as they are replaced.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1275">Pour plus d’informations, consultez [Utiliser un transformateur de paramètre pour personnaliser le remplacement des jetons](/aspnet/core/mvc/controllers/routing#use-a-parameter-transformer-to-customize-token-replacement).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1275">For more information, see [Use a parameter transformer to customize token replacement](/aspnet/core/mvc/controllers/routing#use-a-parameter-transformer-to-customize-token-replacement).</span></span>
* <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1276">RazorLes pages possèdent la `Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.ApplicationModels.PageRouteTransformerConvention` Convention d’API.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1276">Razor Pages has the `Microsoft.AspNetCore.Mvc.ApplicationModels.PageRouteTransformerConvention` API convention.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1277">Cette Convention applique un transformateur de paramètre spécifié à toutes les Razor pages découvertes automatiquement.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1277">This convention applies a specified parameter transformer to all automatically discovered Razor Pages.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1278">Le transformateur de paramètres transforme les segments de nom de fichier et de dossier des Razor itinéraires de pages.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1278">The parameter transformer transforms the folder and file name segments of Razor Pages routes.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1279">Pour plus d’informations, consultez [Utiliser un transformateur de paramètre pour personnaliser les routages de pages](/aspnet/core/razor-pages/razor-pages-conventions#use-a-parameter-transformer-to-customize-page-routes).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1279">For more information, see [Use a parameter transformer to customize page routes](/aspnet/core/razor-pages/razor-pages-conventions#use-a-parameter-transformer-to-customize-page-routes).</span></span>

## <a name="url-generation-reference"></a><span data-ttu-id="d429d-1280">Informations de référence sur la génération d’URL</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1280">URL generation reference</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d429d-1281">L’exemple suivant montre comment générer un lien vers une route selon un dictionnaire de valeurs de route et un <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteCollection> données.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1281">The following example shows how to generate a link to a route given a dictionary of route values and a <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.RouteCollection>.</span></span>

[!code-csharp[](routing/samples/2.x/RoutingSample/Startup.cs?name=snippet_Dictionary)]

<span data-ttu-id="d429d-1282">Le <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathData.VirtualPath> généré à la fin de l’exemple précédent est `/package/create/123`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1282">The <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathData.VirtualPath> generated at the end of the preceding sample is `/package/create/123`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1283">Le dictionnaire fournit les valeurs de route `operation` et `id` du modèle « Suivi de package de route », `package/{operation}/{id}`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1283">The dictionary supplies the `operation` and `id` route values of the "Track Package Route" template, `package/{operation}/{id}`.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1284">Pour plus d’informations, consultez l’exemple de code dans la section [Utilisation du middleware de routage](#use-routing-middleware) ou l’[exemple d’application](https://github.com/dotnet/AspNetCore.Docs/tree/master/aspnetcore/fundamentals/routing/samples).</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1284">For details, see the sample code in the [Use Routing Middleware](#use-routing-middleware) section or the [sample app](https://github.com/dotnet/AspNetCore.Docs/tree/master/aspnetcore/fundamentals/routing/samples).</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d429d-1285">Le deuxième paramètre pour le constructeur <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathContext> est une collection de *valeurs ambiantes*.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1285">The second parameter to the <xref:Microsoft.AspNetCore.Routing.VirtualPathContext> constructor is a collection of *ambient values*.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1286">Les valeurs ambiantes sont pratiques à utiliser, car elles limitent le nombre de valeurs qu’un développeur doit spécifier dans un contexte de requête.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1286">Ambient values are convenient to use because they limit the number of values a developer must specify within a request context.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1287">Les valeurs de route actuelles de la requête actuelle sont considérées comme des valeurs ambiantes pour la génération de liens.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1287">The current route values of the current request are considered ambient values for link generation.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1288">Dans l’action `About` de `HomeController` d’une application ASP.NET Core MVC, vous n’avez pas besoin de spécifier la valeur de route du contrôleur pour créer un lien vers l’action `Index` : la valeur ambiante de `Home` est utilisée.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1288">In an ASP.NET Core MVC app's `About` action of the `HomeController`, you don't need to specify the controller route value to link to the `Index` action&mdash;the ambient value of `Home` is used.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d429d-1289">Les valeurs ambiantes qui ne correspondent pas à un paramètre sont ignorées.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1289">Ambient values that don't match a parameter are ignored.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1290">Les valeurs ambiantes sont également ignorées quand une valeur explicitement fournie remplace la valeur ambiante.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1290">Ambient values are also ignored when an explicitly provided value overrides the ambient value.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1291">La mise en correspondance se produit de gauche à droite dans l’URL.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1291">Matching occurs from left to right in the URL.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d429d-1292">Les valeurs fournies explicitement mais qui n’ont pas de correspondance avec un segment de la route sont ajoutées à la chaîne de requête.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1292">Values explicitly provided but that don't match a segment of the route are added to the query string.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1293">Le tableau suivant présente le résultat en cas d’utilisation du modèle de routage `{controller}/{action}/{id?}`.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1293">The following table shows the result when using the route template `{controller}/{action}/{id?}`.</span></span>

| <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1294">Valeurs ambiantes</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1294">Ambient Values</span></span>                     | <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1295">Valeurs explicites</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1295">Explicit Values</span></span>                        | <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1296">Résultat</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1296">Result</span></span>                  |
| ---------------------------------- | -------------------------------------- | ----------------------- |
| <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1297">controller = "Home"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1297">controller = "Home"</span></span>                | <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1298">action = "About"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1298">action = "About"</span></span>                       | `/Home/About`           |
| <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1299">controller = "Home"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1299">controller = "Home"</span></span>                | <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1300">controller = "Order", action = "About"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1300">controller = "Order", action = "About"</span></span> | `/Order/About`          |
| <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1301">controller = "Home", color = "Red"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1301">controller = "Home", color = "Red"</span></span> | <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1302">action = "About"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1302">action = "About"</span></span>                       | `/Home/About`           |
| <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1303">controller = "Home"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1303">controller = "Home"</span></span>                | <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1304">action = "About", color = "Red"</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1304">action = "About", color = "Red"</span></span>        | `/Home/About?color=Red` |

<span data-ttu-id="d429d-1305">Si une route a une valeur par défaut qui ne correspond pas à un paramètre et que cette valeur est explicitement fournie, elle doit correspondre à la valeur par défaut :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1305">If a route has a default value that doesn't correspond to a parameter and that value is explicitly provided, it must match the default value:</span></span>

```csharp
routes.MapRoute("blog_route", "blog/{*slug}",
    defaults: new { controller = "Blog", action = "ReadPost" });
```

<span data-ttu-id="d429d-1306">La génération de liens génère un lien pour cette route seulement quand les valeurs correspondantes pour `controller` et pour `action` sont fournies.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1306">Link generation only generates a link for this route when the matching values for `controller` and `action` are provided.</span></span>

## <a name="complex-segments"></a><span data-ttu-id="d429d-1307">Segments complexes</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1307">Complex segments</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d429d-1308">Les segments complexes (par exemple, `[Route("/x{token}y")]`) sont traités par la mise en correspondance des littéraux de droite à gauche de manière non gourmande.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1308">Complex segments (for example `[Route("/x{token}y")]`) are processed by matching up literals from right to left in a non-greedy way.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1309">Consultez [ce code](https://github.com/dotnet/AspNetCore/blob/release/2.2/src/Http/Routing/src/Patterns/RoutePatternMatcher.cs#L293) pour obtenir une explication détaillée de la façon dont les segments complexes sont mis en correspondance.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1309">See [this code](https://github.com/dotnet/AspNetCore/blob/release/2.2/src/Http/Routing/src/Patterns/RoutePatternMatcher.cs#L293) for a detailed explanation of how complex segments are matched.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1310">[L’exemple de code](https://github.com/dotnet/AspNetCore/blob/release/2.2/src/Http/Routing/src/Patterns/RoutePatternMatcher.cs#L293) n’est pas utilisé par ASP.NET Core, mais il fournit une bonne explication des segments complexes.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1310">The [code sample](https://github.com/dotnet/AspNetCore/blob/release/2.2/src/Http/Routing/src/Patterns/RoutePatternMatcher.cs#L293) is not used by ASP.NET Core, but it provides a good explanation of complex segments.</span></span>

::: moniker range="< aspnetcore-2.2"

<span data-ttu-id="d429d-1311">Le routage est responsable du mappage des URI des requêtes aux gestionnaires de routage et de la distribution des requêtes entrantes.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1311">Routing is responsible for mapping request URIs to route handlers and dispatching an incoming requests.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1312">Les routes sont définies dans l’application et configurées au démarrage de l’application.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1312">Routes are defined in the app and configured when the app starts.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1313">Une route peut éventuellement extraire des valeurs de l’URL contenue dans la requête, et ces valeurs peuvent ensuite être utilisées pour le traitement de la requête.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1313">A route can optionally extract values from the URL contained in the request, and these values can then be used for request processing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1314">En utilisant des routes configurées à partir de l’application, le routage est en mesure de générer des URL qui mappent à des gestionnaires de routage.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1314">Using configured routes from the app, routing is able to generate URLs that map to route handlers.</span></span>

<span data-ttu-id="d429d-1315">Pour utiliser les scénarios de routage les plus récents dans ASP.NET Core 2.1, spécifiez la [version de compatibilité](xref:mvc/compatibility-version) à l’inscription des services MVC dans `Startup.ConfigureServices` :</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1315">To use the latest routing scenarios in ASP.NET Core 2.1, specify the [compatibility version](xref:mvc/compatibility-version) to the MVC services registration in `Startup.ConfigureServices`:</span></span>

```csharp
services.AddMvc()
    .SetCompatibilityVersion(CompatibilityVersion.Version_2_1);
```

> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1316">Ce document traite du routage ASP.NET Core de bas niveau.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1316">This document covers low-level ASP.NET Core routing.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1317">Pour plus d’informations sur le routage ASP.NET Core MVC, consultez <xref:mvc/controllers/routing>.</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1317">For information on ASP.NET Core MVC routing, see <xref:mvc/controllers/routing>.</span></span> <span data-ttu-id="d429d-1318">Pour plus d’informations sur les conventions de routage dans les Razor pages, consultez <xref:razor-pages/razor-pages-conventions> .</span><span class="sxs-lookup"><span data-stu-id="d429d-1318">For information on routing conventions in Razor Pages, see <xref:razor-pages/razor-pages-conventions>.</span></span>
